The goal of the game is to have more pieces of your color than your opponent.\r\n\r\nDownload and play now!\r\n\r\n\r\n‚òÖ ‚òÖ ‚òÖ FEATURES ‚òÖ ‚òÖ ‚òÖ \r\n‚úì challenging AI opponent\r\n‚úì intuitive interface\r\n‚úì fluid gameplay\r\n\r\n‚òÖ ‚òÖ ‚òÖ TIPS & RULES ‚òÖ ‚òÖ ‚òÖ \r\n‚úì You play with black and you are the first to make a move. \r\n‚úì The game alternates between your turn and the opponent's turn.\r\n‚úì At the start of your turn, you are presented with a number of allowed moves lighthearted with green disks. Pick one piece and then tap on one of the suggested square.\r\n‚úì If between the displayed choice and your black piece, there are only white pieces the move is valid.\r\n‚úì The pieces you capture can be positioned on a vertical line, a horizontal line and a diagonal line.\r\n‚úì If you or your opponent run out of allowed moves, the game will end.
